\xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd (\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81. \xd0\xa3\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c-\xd0\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd0\xba) \xe2\x80\x94 \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xba\xd3\x99\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbf, \xd0\xbc\xd3\x99\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd3\x99\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b. \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96 1720 \xd0\xb6 \xd0\x95\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd1\x81 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\xae\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb1\xd1\x96 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd.\n

1917 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd-\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd2\xb1\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x91\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x9e\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x82\xd3\xa9\xd1\x80\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 \xd0\xaf\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd0\x92\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87 \xd0\xa3\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x88\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1918 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 14 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b \xd0\xba\xd2\xaf\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd1\x88\xd1\x82\xd1\x96.\n

1918 \xd0\xb6.- \xe2\x80\x9c \xd0\xa3\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c-\xd0\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c\xe2\x80\x9d \xd0\xb3\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96 \xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b.\n

1919 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x87\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\xd0\x9d.\xd0\xa2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd1\x84\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xa1.\xd0\x93\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd1\x87\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe \xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1919 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xba\xd2\xaf\xd0\xb7 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb4\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x96. \xd0\x91\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96 \xd0\x90\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd2\x9a\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb \xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xba\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xba \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82 \xd0\x9d\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x98\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87 \xd0\xa2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd1\x84\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1920 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb5\xd2\xa3\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\x9a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96 \xd0\x90\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x9a\xd0\xb5\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81 \xd2\xaf\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1920 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 4 \xd1\x81\xd3\x99\xd1\x83\xd1\x96\xd1\x80 \xd0\xba\xd2\xaf\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96 \xd0\xa5\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd2\xae\xd0\xb9\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x91\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

1924 \xd0\xb6.- \xd0\x91\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x84\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x96 \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\x9a\xd0\xb5\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1925 \xd0\xb6.- \xd0\x91-4 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbf\xd1\x82\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x88 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1930 \xd0\xb6., \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xe2\x80\x93 \xd0\xa1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd3\x99\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb-\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x84\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd2\xb1\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x91\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb-\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xbd\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96\xd1\x80 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd1\x8f\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 20 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x84\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1931 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa0\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd1\x86\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0-\xd0\xa0\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96\xd1\x80-\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. 1938 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb \xd0\x9a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96 \xd0\x90\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa2\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\x9e\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x90\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1934 \xd0\xb6. \xe2\x80\x93 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xa1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9a\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96. \xd0\x9e\xd0\xbb \xd2\xaf\xd1\x88 \xd0\xba\xd2\xaf\xd0\xbd \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x9e\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x91\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\x9a\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96. 1934 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\x9a\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd1\x81\xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7 \xd1\x81\xd3\xa9\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd2\x93\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82 (\xd0\xb1\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\x90\xd1\x82\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x83 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96) \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd1\x80 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x85\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd1\x88 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1935 \xd0\xb6.- \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd3\x99\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb0\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc \xd0\x93\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8c\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

1939 \xd0\xb6.- \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd1\x81\xd1\x83-\xd1\x8d\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x80 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1941 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 8 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xba\xd2\xaf\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb5\xd2\xa3\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x96\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x96 \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b, \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b, \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1949 \xd0\xb6.- \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd2\xae\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb1\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1950 \xd0\xb6.- \xd0\x9c\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbb \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x83 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

1950 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb \xe2\x80\x93 \xd1\x82\xd2\xaf\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8- \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x83 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\x90\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x84\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b - \xe2\x80\x9c\xd0\x93\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x86\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xe2\x80\x9d- \xe2\x80\x9c \xd0\x90\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x86\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xe2\x80\x9d. 1955 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa2\xd2\xaf\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\x91\xd2\xaf\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83-\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.( \xd0\x92\xd0\x9d\xd0\x98\xd0\x98\xd1\x86\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82)\n

1951 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb- \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 \xd2\xaf\xd0\xb9\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

1951 \xd0\xb6. \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd-\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd1\x88 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1952 \xd0\xb6, \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc- \xd2\x9a\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xba\xd3\x99\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1952 \xd0\xb6. 20 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xe2\x80\x93 \xd0\x93\xd0\xad\xd0\xa1 \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd2\xa3\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x88 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba \xd2\x9b\xd1\x83\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

1953 \xd0\xb6. 3 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc- \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd1\x81\xd1\x83-\xd1\x8d\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x80 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd2\xa3\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x88 \xd1\x88\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8e\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

\xd0\x9c\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1954 \xd0\xb6. \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd2\xa3\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x97\xd0\xb0\xd1\x89\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0-\xd0\x97\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd2\xb1\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1955 \xd0\xb6. \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc. \xd0\x96\xd0\xb0\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd3\xa8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd2\xaf\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd3\x99\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd3\x99\xd0\xb9\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb \xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x85\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

1956 \xd0\xb6., 19 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc - \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd2\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7 \xd1\x84\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

1957 \xd0\xb6, 30 \xd1\x81\xd3\x99\xd1\x83\xd1\x96\xd1\x80 - \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbc\xd3\x99\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb0\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1958 \xd0\xb6., 15 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7 - \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd2\xa3\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x88 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd2\xb1\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b, \xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd2\xaf\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b.\n

1958 \xd0\xb6., \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd- \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81- \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb0\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1958 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

(5100 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd)\n

1970 \xd0\xb6., \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd2\xa3\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xe2\x80\x93 \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\x9c\xd3\x99\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x83, \xd0\x90\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

1970 \xd0\xb6., 9 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7 - \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\x95\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd1\x81 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd3\xa9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbf\xd1\x96\xd1\x80 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

1970., \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd - \xe2\x80\x9c\xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xe2\x80\x9d \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd2\xaf\xd0\xb9\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

1970., \xd1\x88\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 - \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd1\x96\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba-\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd1\x84\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1973., \xd1\x81\xd3\x99\xd1\x83\xd1\x96\xd1\x80 - \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b: \xd2\xae\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb1\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\x9e\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8c \xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b.\n

1974 \xd0\xb6., \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0 \xe2\x80\x93 \xd0\x96\xd0\xb0\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xa1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\x9a\xd0\x9e\xd0\x9a\xd0\x9f \xd0\xa5\xd0\xa5\xd0\x86\xd0\x86\xd0\x86 \xd1\x81\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1975., 7 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80 - \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\x95\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd1\x81 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd2\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\x9e\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd1\x88 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1975., \xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xba\xd2\xaf\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba - \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbc\xd3\x99\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8-\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x83 \xd1\x83\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1979\xd0\xb6., \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xe2\x80\x93 \xd0\x96\xd1\x96\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba \xe2\x80\x93\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 500 \xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\xaf\xd1\x88\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb5\xd2\xa3\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1980 \xd0\xb6., \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80 \xe2\x80\x93 \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd1\x88\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b: \xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\x9a\xd2\xaf\xd1\x80\xd1\x88\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc, \xd0\xa2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9, \xd0\x9c\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbb, \xe2\x80\x9c \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xe2\x80\x9d \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

1981., \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0 \xe2\x80\x93 \xd0\x9e.\xd0\x91\xd3\xa9\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xe2\x80\x9c \xd3\x98\xd0\xbd \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b \xd1\x88\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xe2\x80\x9d \xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b.\n

1992.\xd2\xaf \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd2\xa3\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 - \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbf\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xa2\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb8\xd1\x86\xd0\xba \xd0\xa5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xe2\x80\x9c\xd0\xa5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81 \xd0\x92\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xe2\x80\x9d \xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1994 \xd0\xb6.,- \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd2\xa3\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 - \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd2\xa3\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x88 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbe\xd2\x9b\xd1\x83 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd0\x93\xd1\x83\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1996 \xd0\xb6., \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd2\xa3\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xe2\x80\x93 70 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd0\xa2\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb8\xd1\x86\xd0\xba \xd0\xa5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1997., \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80 \xe2\x80\x93 \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xa1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96. \xd2\x9a\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xba\xd2\xaf\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x9a\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8c\xd1\x81\xd0\xba \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b \xd0\x9c\xd2\xb1\xd1\x85\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd3\x98\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96. \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd1\x80 \xd0\x9c.\xd3\x98\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\xa3\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd0\xa7\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8f\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xb8\xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb \xd0\x98\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87, 1917\xd0\xb6.\xd1\x82., \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80, \xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd,\xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\x9e\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbc\xd2\xaf\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x96.\xd0\x96\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.\n

\xd0\x98\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd0\x90\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa1\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87, 1928., \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b, \xe2\x80\x9c\xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xe2\x80\x9d, \xe2\x80\x9c\xd0\xa2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c\xe2\x80\x9d, \xe2\x80\x9c \xd0\x92\xd0\xb5\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xe2\x80\x9d \xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd0\x91\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xae\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x92\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87, \xd0\x94.\xd0\xa1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xe2\x80\x93\xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x85\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b. \xd0\xae. \xd0\x92.\xd0\x91\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81-\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb5\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbe\xd2\x9b\xd1\x83 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd0\x9c\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2 \xd0\x95\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd0\x90\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87, 1937 \xd0\xb6.\xd1\x82., \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xe2\x80\x93\xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x95\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd3\x98\xd0\xbb\xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\xb1\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb \xd0\xbe\xd2\x9b\xd1\x83 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf \xd0\xba\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd0\xa8\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f\xd1\x85\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd0\x91\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82 \xd0\x9c\xd1\x83\xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87, \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb6\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd-\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd3\xa9\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x96. \xd0\x9a\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b 90 \xe2\x80\x93 \xd1\x88\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd1\x8d\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd0\x9f\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x90\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x95\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87, 1936 \xd0\xb6.\xd1\x82., \xd0\x95\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd1\x81 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd. \xd0\x9e\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xa1\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x82 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b, \xd0\x9e\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\x9c\xd3\x99\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd2\xaf\xd0\xb9\xd1\x96, \xd0\x95\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd1\x81 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9a\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb \xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b, \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf, \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b, \xd1\x83\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80, \xd2\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\x9e\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd1\x88 \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd0\x9a\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\x98\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0, 1927\xd0\xb6.\xd1\x82., \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81 \xd1\x85\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3, \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81 \xd0\xb4\xd3\x99\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b . \xd0\x9c\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\x98\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83 \xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd.\n

\xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x9a\xd0\xa1\xd0\xa0\xd0\x9e \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd0\x9a\xd0\xb5\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd1\x88\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\x91\xd2\xaf\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8-\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x83 \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83-\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd 1950 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8-\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x83 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd-\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd1\x82\xd2\xaf\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb6\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96 (\xd0\x92\xd0\x9d\xd0\x98\xd0\x98\xd1\x86\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82).\n

\xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x9d\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x90\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xc2\xab\xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xc2\xbb \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xc2\xab\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x98\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xc2\xbb \xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0, \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xb8\xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb \xd0\xa7\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8f\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd3\xa9\xd2\xa3\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 VII \xd1\x84\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b \xd3\xa9\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x96. \xd0\x9c\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\x94\xd3\x99\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd0\xa1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa8\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x85\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b (\xd3\xa8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81
